Gajde(Gayda) or Bagpipe is a Celtic instrument originating in Ireland. The Celts introduced it to Illyrians when they went down to Southern Europe and Balkans. The Illryian(Balkan) Gayda is similar to the Celtic-Irish Bagpipe, but it's not the same. I see comments people saying it's Serbian, Romanian, Albanian, Greek instrument. It's not! Gayda is Illyrian.
